<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orijentácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентация.html>ориента́ций</a></b>)

<li>direction of attention

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ориентироваться.html>ориенти́роваться</a> (8748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ориентировать.html>ориенти́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orijentírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орошать.html>ороша́ть</a> (29745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ороси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орошать.html>ороша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orošátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ороси́ть</b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орт.html>орт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ort</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орт.html>о́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орт.html>о́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орт.html>о́ртов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit of vector length</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crosscut, cross drift (horizontal underground excavation with no direct exit to the surface)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cocaine</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:христианин.html>христиани́н</a>! ― <a href = vnd.unilang:вскричать.html>вскрича́л</a> Аванес. <a href = vnd.unilang:дворянин.html>Дворяни́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:армянин.html>армя́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почти.html>почти́</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ортодокс.html>ортодо́ксы</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показать.html>показа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> малообразованным, <a href = vnd.unilang:добавить.html>доба́вил</a>: ― <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>И́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:милый.html>ми́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:требоваться.html>тре́буется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сское</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>Хо́чешь</a> Василису ― <a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́йся</a> Иваном! <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зках</a>! </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a> (1813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orǫdьje</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orúdije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tool, instrument, implement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труда́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>orúdije</b> trudá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">tool for labor</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gun, cannon, artillery piece</li></ol>

***орудовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:орудовать.html>ору́довать</a> (9355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orúdije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудовать.html>ору́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orúdovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work <i>(with)</i>, to handle, to manipulate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орудовать.html>ору́довать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:топор.html>топоро́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lóvko <b>orúdovatʹ</b> toporóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to know how to use (handle expertly) an axe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be active
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:орудовать.html>ору́довал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опытный.html>о́пытный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жулик.html>жу́лик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ <b>orúdoval</b> ópytnyj žúlik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an experienced thief has been at work here</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́дие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">orúdije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оруди́йний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">orudíjnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">orúžije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружейный.html>оруже́йный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oružéjnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружейник.html>оруже́йник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oružéjnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***оружие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a> (666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">орѫжиѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orǫžije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orǫžьje</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orǫga</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orǫžь</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">orúžije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>weapon(s), arm(s)</li>
<li>cold steel</li></ol>

***осадить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:осадить.html>осади́ть</a> (9666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадить.html>осади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осаживать.html>оса́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to check, to rein in, to rein back</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take down a peg</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадок.html>оса́дка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osádka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадок.html>оса́док</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osádok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оса́дочный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osádočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиоактивный.html>радиоакти́вные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осадок.html>оса́дки</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">radioaktívnyje osádki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадить.html>осади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осаждать.html>осажда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lay siege <i>(to)</i>, to besiege, to beset, to beleaguer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:осадить.html>осади́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крепость.html>кре́пость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>osadítʹ</b> krépostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay siege to a fortress; besiege a fortress</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pester <i>(with)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осада.html>оса́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osáda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадный.html>оса́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осадить.html>осади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">osadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осаждать.html>осажда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to precipitate</li></ol>
